---

### Summary of `README.md`

`README.md` is the main entry point for users and developers.
Key points:

1. **Project Overview**  Consoul is an AIpowered terminal assistant with a rich TUI, CLI, and SDK. It supports multiple providers (Claude, GPT4, Gemini, Ollama, LlamaCpp) and can run models locally.

2. **Quick Start**  Install with `pip install consoul`, set an API key (`ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`, `OPENAI_API_KEY`, or `GOOGLE_API_KEY`), and launch via `consoul` or use the SDK (`Consoul()`).

3. **Features**  Beautiful TUI, multiprovider support, AIpowered tools for file editing, code search, image analysis, web search, session management.

4. **CLI & SDK**  Demonstrates how to use the command line (`consoul chat`, `consoul ask`) and the Python SDK for embedding Consoul into applications.

5. **Documentation Links**  Directs to full docs, configuration, TUI guides, tools, and SDK sections.

6. **Configuration**  Example `~/.consoul/config.yaml` shows model and tool settings, including permission policies and conversation history options.

7. **Security**  Highlights permission policies, approval workflows, audit logging, and command validation. Points to `SECURITY.md` for details.

8. **Contributing & License**  Standard MIT license, welcoming contributions.

Overall, the README presents Consoul as an extensible, secure, AIaugmented terminal tool, providing clear instructions for installation, usage, and further customization., has_tool_calls_in_message=[], full_response_len=4164, cancelled=False
